msg:Checking inn was easy. My daughter was able to view the lobby area comfortably while we waited for our passports to be processed. Our room was on the first floor of the C wing. It was multi level suite. The hallway had a damp musty smell, but it did not follow you into the room. The air conditioners worked and kept the suite cool downstairs while upstairs to cool down comfortably for bed time you needed to close the bedroom door. What we enjoyed the most was the location, across the street from the beach with easy gate access a short walk away. Perfect late night snack was from the coca cola stand with American hotdogs and burgers. The pool was refreshing and the ocean breeze can been felt. As for amenities, the pool lacks the attraction for children that other beachfront hotels has but my daughter did not seem to mind. Staff was always helpful for our needs during our stay and finding taxi services was always quick. Just 15 minutes drive to nearby shopping malls and late night snack street which was a big hit for our family! We will definitely come again.
